colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text setting\nis correctly translated to 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' on Qt 6.4,\nwhereas it should be 'TextBrightnessThreshold' on earlier Qt versions.\n\nBUG DESCRIPTION:\n===============\nWhen users configure the dark mode text brightness threshold setting\n(`colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text`) and qutebrowser is running\nwith Qt version 6.4, the setting has no effect on dark mode rendering.\n\nROOT CAUSE:\n===========\nIn Qt 6.4, Chromium renamed the DarkMode setting 'TextBrightnessThreshold'\nto 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'. If qutebrowser continues to use the\nold 'TextBrightnessThreshold' key when talking to Chromium on Qt 6.4,\nChromium will not recognize it and the setting will be ignored.\n\nThe qutebrowser code has a copy_replace_setting() method that's supposed to\nhandle this rename for Qt 6.4. If this method is not called, or if it doesn't\nactually replace the key, then the setting will use the wrong Chromium key name\nand Chromium will ignore it.\n\nTEST STRATEGY:\n==============\nThis test extracts just the darkmode.py setting definitions and logic,\nand verifies that:\n1.
